name:Tâ€aâ€iâ€dâ€iâ€xâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€xâ€iâ€oâ€nâ€g
info:Deluxe Family Room
info:Stayed in May 2023
info:Family
info:5 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 4, 2023
msg:Come on May 1, 2023.

Because I came to Huishan Ancient Town to play, I wanted to choose a hotel nearby. After a comprehensive evaluation, I feel that this hotel is the most suitable. There are several advantages:

1. Location. The hotel is only a 10-minute drive from Huishan Ancient Town, which is very convenient in the past, which is especially suitable for travelers who come to Huishan by car.

2. Hardware. The hotel only opened in 2018. The room type is good, the hardware is relatively new, and the environment is very clean. It is conceivable to see the local people in Wuxi holding wedding banquets here.

3. Catering. The hotel's buffet breakfast is in the cafeteria on the top floor. The entire level is a dining area. The breakfast variety is relatively complete, and the taste is not bad. It is worthy of the hotel's star rating.

4. Periphery. The Baile Plaza where the hotel is located is one of the top commercial complexes in Wuxi. There are quite a variety of businesses in various formats, and it is a very good place for leisure and entertainment.

5. Price. Based on the above points, the price of the hotel is relatively not particularly high. As a tourist from Shanghai, I really think this price/performance ratio is still acceptable.

6. Stop. The hotel shares parking spaces with other businesses in Park Plaza, and the number is sufficient. Before going out every time, you can get the electronic parking coupon at the front desk of the hotel to deduct the parking fee, which is very practical.
